          <article class="clearfix post-27342 page type-page status-publish hentry" id="post-27342">
           <header class="entry-header">
            <h1 class="entry-title">
             Faculty
            </h1>
           </header>
           <!-- .entry-header -->
           <div class="entry-content">
            <div class="panel-layout" id="pl-27342">
             <div class="panel-grid panel-no-style" id="pg-27342-0">
              <div class="panel-grid-cell" id="pgc-27342-0-0">
               <div class="so-panel widget widget_black-studio-tinymce widget_black_studio_tinymce panel-first-child panel-last-child" data-index="0" id="panel-27342-0-0-0">
                <div class="textwidget">
                 <p>
                  The College of Engineering offers a robust learning and research environment, and set of opportunities in a multitude of majors. Our world class faculty members are pioneers in the engineering community and are very passionate about developing the next generation of scholars, leaders, students and professionals.
                 </p>
                </div>
               </div>
              </div>

      function adjustImages() {
        jQuery('.person-image').each(function(index, element) {
            var imgWidth = jQuery(this).find('img').width();
            var imgHeight = jQuery(this).find('img').height();
            var width = jQuery(this).width();
            //jQuery(this).height(width);
            jQuery(this).css('display', 'block');
        });
    };
    jQuery(window).resize(function() {
        adjustImages();
    });
    jQuery(window).load(function() {
        adjustImages();
    });
